- **Rate Set:** 400 bps
- **Reasoning:** By lowering the rate to 400 bps, I aim to become more competitive in the market, particularly in light of the average market rate being higher at 467 bps. This aggressive pricing strategy aligns with my goal to gain market share, and I believe it will attract more consumers while still allowing for a sustainable profit margin above my cost of funds.
- **Expected Outcome:** I anticipate capturing around 10-12% of the market share with this rate, leading to an increase in profit, potentially exceeding $1,500,000.
